I havn‚Äôt had the coffee but every time I‚Äôm in there people are getting it. Good sign. They have energy drinks too if you don‚Äôt like coffee.  My daughter loves the pink with sprinkles donut. < Review>
Had to rent a compact car at the last minute and called the location to see if one was available.  Was given a quote for $299 per week but when I arrived at the office, the contract had been revised to $229 per week.  This lower price was confirmed by the employee in person.  When I returned the car, the rental rate had been changed back to $299.  After haggling with the manager, she "met me half way" and took $35 off the total price.  Now looking on line at the weekly rental prices offered, I feel rather ripped off.  The same car (Nissan Versa) is available on line for $108 per week.  Nice car, pleasant employees and very convenient pick up/drop off but dicey on pricing.  Learn from my lesson, shop on line and do your research before agreeing to a price.  If I go back, I will certainly see what the on line rates are first.</Review>

<user>101513893934091114670</user>< Name>
Mako J< /Name>
<Time>1521328244486<//Time>< rating>
4< /rating>
< Text>
This place is really old, but it's a lot of fun for kids. If they upgraded some of their seating area and decor, it would make a world of difference.

The Golden Skate is especially good for birthday parties. When you have one there, they take care of Pizza, cake, serving and cleanup.  It's not cheap, but it makes things very easy for parents.

Note that if you bring your own roller blades or skates, make sure you have wheels that are somewhat hard.  I used to play roller hockey and I have wheels rated at 72A.  The Golden State has a painted smooth surface, so I literally could not stop, my wheels would not skid at all, so it felt sticky to skate on their surface.  I have a set of outdoor wheels that are 85A and I think they would have been much better for this place.< /Text>

< Review>
Every other month our family gets together for some type of activity.  This time we chose The Golden Skate. The music selection was not exciting and the music was too slow most times. The atmosphere was fun, the staff were friendly and the No sagging pants rules were good and funny. Their website and phone instructions were misleading and if you aren't careful you'll get ripped off.  Their website states that there is a $13 admission fee whether you skate or not. The cashier only asks you how many people not how many people are skating. We had a group of 8 adults and 5 children. After speaking with the manager we were refunded our admission fee for 4 adults. And the snack bar prices were extremely high priced and cash only! However, you can pay the entrance fee with credit.</Review>

The Golden Skate is a great place for younger kids to have fun and get some exercise at the same time!  I take my daughters there regularly (aged 10 and 13) and we always have a good time.  The owner has made many improvements in the last year or two -- and we have never had a negative experience there.  We usually attend the 6:30-9 sessions where there are younger kids.  The 9-11 sessions tend to have an older crowd.  Don't usually go to the early sessions, but I've heard they are good for beginners.  Come check it out!< /text>

<Review>A good place to go if you have no where else with a smooth floor to skate. It's a pretty small rink so it gets kind of crowded, especially on Sundays. A lot of really little kids, which is great if you have kids, but if you're an adult it's a bit of a challenge trying to dodge all the little ones - either stopping or going the wrong direction. It has the same feel as a bowling alley, a little dingey and under staffed, but it works. Dress code is also a little strict. No midrift showing allowed, no hats. They have both rollerskates and rollerblades to rent. 13$ for entry and $5 for skate rental. Also make sure to bring lots of quarters if you plan on using the little cubbies for your stuff (your outside shoes,wallet, keys,ect.)< /Review>< username>
Bug< /username>
